<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старина.html>старина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stariná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starínnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>antique, ancient, olden, age-old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>starínnaja</b> mébelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>antique</b> furniture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>starínnyj</b> zámok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ancient</b> castle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нной</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>starínnoj</b> žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the <b>olden</b> days</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>old <span class="use-with-mention">e.g. of relationships</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">my s nim <b>starínnyje</b> prijáteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he and I are <b>old</b> friends</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>стари́ннее, стари́нней.</i>

***стародавний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стародавний.html>старода́вний</a> (28705)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>ста</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ний</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2*a-.
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. предположительна.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starostь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ostь</i>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старт.html>старт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">start</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stártovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> starting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovyj</b> pistolét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starting/starter's pistol</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>launching
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:площадка.html>площа́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovaja</b> ploščádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">launch pad</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>initial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитал.html>капита́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovyj</b> kapitál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">initial capital</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́вия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovyje</b> uslóvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starting position</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стартовый.html>ста́ртовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:битый.html>бит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stártovyj</b> bit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">start bit</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>ста</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ру́ш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-стар-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-уш-к</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старческий.html>ста́рческий</a> (8121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-českij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старческий.html>ста́рческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stárčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> old age, senile</li>
<li>of monastic elders</li></ol>

***старший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a> (615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáršij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>elder, older, senior</li>
<li>eldest, oldest</li>
<li>higher, highest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> first (lieutenant)</li>
<li>senior (suffix used for names of elders)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáršij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́ршего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́ршие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рших</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foreman</li>
<li>chief, man in charge</li></ol>

***старый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a> (185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">старъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)старе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>old</li>
<li>ancient, antique</li>
<li>olden</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The end-stressed short neuter form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>старо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staró</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used with the meaning "long-known" (of news, information, etc.), and in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>старо́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éto <b>staró</b> kak mir</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it's as <b>old</b> as the world</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; otherwise, the stem-stressed form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́ро</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is preferred.</li></ul>
<p><i>Comparatives (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ста́рше and (<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)старе́е:</i>
</p>
<ul><li>The comparative forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are used for comparing age or rank, e.g.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a> ста́рше <a href = vnd.unilang:девочка.html>де́вочки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Málʹčik stárše dévočki na dva góda.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The boy is older than the girl by two years</span></div>. The forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">старе́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staréje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">постаре́е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postaréje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are used when both objects of comparison are "old", e.g.</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>стари́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>стано́вится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> старе́е <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> старе́е.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Starík stanóvitsja vsjó staréje i staréje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The old man is getting older and older.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Some sources claim that <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поста́рше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">postárše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are only comparatives of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старший.html>ста́рший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáršij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">elder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is itself originally an adjectival comparative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">встарь</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vstarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">исстари</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">isstari</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

Катаев</a>, «<a href = vnd.unilang:миллион.html>Миллио́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ний</a>», <span class="example-date">1930</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>г</a>.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></i></span></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:храм.html>Храм</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заставленный.html>заста́влен</a> жертвенниками, многорукими <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́туями</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:этажерка.html>этаже́рками</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:груда.html>гру́дами</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:статуэтка.html>статуэ́ток</a></span> бодисатв. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%95%D1%84%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%BC%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%98%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BD_%D0%90%D0%BD%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Ефремов, Иван Антонович"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***стать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a> (11761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand, become</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stand</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">statʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>станови́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand in a certain location or near someone or something (interchangeable with <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>Ста́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ешься</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stanʹ</b> ko mne, a to poterjáješʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand near me so you don't get lost.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>Ста́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мно́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ешься</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stanʹ</b> so mnóju, a to poterjáješʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand near me so you don't get lost.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> побли́же.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> poblíže.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Get closer.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> лу́чше <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдруг.html>вдруг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосулька.html>сосу́льки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упаду́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> lúčše sjudá, a to vdrug sosúlʹki upadút.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Better stand here in case icicles suddenly fall.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́чередь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́череди</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпи́те</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> v óčeredʹ, molodój čelovék! Vy ne dólgo v óčeredi že búdete stojátʹ, poterpíte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand in the queue, young man! You won't be standing in the queue for long, have some patience.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́нут</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́с</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánut</b> li gonjátʹ oní krýs?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Will</b> they <b>start</b> chasing the rats?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> pisátʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>began</b> to write.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> pitʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>took</b> to drinking.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in negative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be not going to; <span class="use-with-mention">used to express a determined negative attitude</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1887</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>), Constance Garnett, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%94%D0%B0%D1%87%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%B8_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Дачники (Чехов)">«<a href = vnd.unilang:темнота.html>Темнота́</a>»</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Darkness_(Chekhov/Garnett)" class="extiw" title="s:Darkness (Chekhov/Garnett)">Darkness</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ше</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благородие.html>благоро́дие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лости</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>на́чал</a> кири́ла. — <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́</a> ва́ську! <a href = vnd.unilang:непременный.html>непреме́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>член</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговаривать.html>разгова́ривать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a>: «<a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>Пошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>вон</a>!»</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Váše blagoródije, ja opjátʹ k tvojéj mílosti! — náčal Kiríla. — Vot s otcóm prišól, sdélaj mílostʹ, otpustí Vásʹku! Nepreménnyj člen razgovárivatʹ <b>ne stal</b>. Govorít: “Pošól <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>von</a>!”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Your honour, I have come again to ask your gracious mercy," began Kirila. "Here I have come with my father. Be merciful, let Vaska go! The permanent member <b>would not</b> talk to me. He said: 'Go away!'"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́ну</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne <b>stánu</b> étovo délatʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m not going to do it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass away

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">statʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>ста́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>build</li>
<li>trait, character, type
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná jemú pod <b>statʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She is a match for him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S kakój <b>státi</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>colloquial</i>) Why should I/you/he/she/it/we/they? For what reason?; why?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 15a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>станови́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ст-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

***статься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a> (15093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">státʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">státʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to become, to happen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́лось</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što s nim <b>stálosʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what has become of him?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">móžet <b>státʹsja</b>, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it may happen that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:вполне.html>вполне́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(vpolné) móžet <b>státʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is (quite) possible/probable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́нется</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s tebjá <b>stánetsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one can well expect that from you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
